id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxCategory_CategoryDescription"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/cz/cz-header2.jpg" alt="CZ Firearms"><p></p> <p><span>CZ has a long history of producing high quality and affordable firearms. &nbsp;CZ has been designing and manufacturing small arms since 1936. &nbsp;Nearly 80 years of experience has resulted in legendary pistol and rifle designs. &nbsp;The CZ 75 has become an icon in the pistol world (searching for Wonder Nine on Wikipedia returns a picture of a CZ 75 B) and it is known for it's timeless design and superb performance. &nbsp;Impact Guns has a wide variety of CZ pistols and Dan Wesson pistols in stock. &nbsp;</span></p> <p><font face="arial,helvetica,sans-serif" size="2">CZ rifles have long been known for their accuracy. &nbsp;This fact is in large part due to the barrels, which undergo a transformation unique in the firearms industry. &nbsp;Whether in the rimfire 455 platform or the highly-prestigous Ultimate Hunting Rifle, you know that you will be getting a very accurate, reliable, high quality firearm. &nbsp;Impact Guns carries a wide variety of CZ rifles, representing one of the best values in hunting today.</font></p> <table border="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%"> <tbody> <tr> <td><a href="../../../../handguns.aspx?Manufacturer=CZ+USA"><img
